 7
 9 Where buildings fall when earthquake on Richter scale 2
 9 richter scale par bukamp aane par halkaa kampan hota he
 Know what the impact can be on the Richter scale according to the intensity of the earthquake: 7
 9 richter scale par bukamp aane par jahaan imaaraten gir jaati hai vahiin 2
 9 On the Richter scale there is a mild vibration when an earthquake occurs
 jaane richter paimaane par bukamp kii tivrata ke hisaab se kya ho saktaa he asar:- 0 se 1
 Seismographs show only when earthquakes occur on the 9 Richter scale
 - 2 se 2
 9 On the Richter scale there is a mild vibration when an earthquake occurs
 - 3 se 3
 9 If there is an earthquake on the Richter scale, a truck passes by you, this is the effect
 - 4 se 4
 9 An earthquake on the Richter scale can break windows
 deevaaron par tange frem gir sakate hai
 - 5 to 5
 9 richter scale par bukamp aane par furniture hill saktaa he
 - 6 to 6
 9 richter scale par bukamp aane par imaaraton kii neenv darak sakati he
 Upper floors may suffer damage
 - 7 se 7
 Buildings collapse when earthquakes occur on the 9 Richter scale
 jameen ke andar pipe fat jate hai
 - 8 to 8
 9 richter scale par bukamp aane par imaaraton sahit bade pul bhi gir jate hai
 - Complete destruction due to earthquake on Richter scale of 9 and above

 As the use of computers and the Internet is increasing in the world, the threat to the Internet is also increasing
 har din hamen nae online khataron se dochaar hona padataa he
 Let's know about the 5 big threats on the Internet and how to avoid these threats
 1
 Virus: Hackers create new viruses and send them to people's computers and mobiles via the Internet
 yah khatarnaak virus bank acount se lekar fasebuk, jimail ke password bhi uda le jate hai
 Thousands of such cases occur every day around the world where hackers use passwords to execute their dangerous plans
 kaise bachein:virus se bachane kaa sabase aasaan tarika apane computer or software ko lagaataar apadet rakhana he
 Avoid using pirated windows and pirated software
 free antiveyras ke bajaae ped antiveyras kaa istemaal karen
 2
 malware:malware kaa matlab vaise software hai jo security veryphid nahin hote hai or aapke computer or mobile ko nuksaan pahunchaate hai
 These software are installed in your device without your knowledge and steal your data
 kaise bachein:inase bachane ke liye aapako koi bhi software inastol karne se pehle kaaphi satark rahane kii jarurat he
 Before installing any software, make sure that it is from the verified publisher or not
 3
 ddos attack: 'denial of service attack' is the most dangerous attack done through internet
 havers is takanic kaa istemaal karke epabiai or mosaad jaisi duniya kii badi suraksha agenciyon kii website tak hack kar chuke hai
 Through this attack, hackers do not steal your data directly but instead increase the traffic of internet and fill any website with spam, which can also steal the data of the person who opens that website
 kaise bachein:ddos atake se bachane ke liye router ke firewal main filtering ko inable kar len
 Always keep the computer firewall on and you can also use a third party firewall
 ddos atake se bachane ke liye aap apane internet sarvice prowider kii bhi madad le sakate hai
 If you want to protect your website from this attack, then you can hire ddos Specialist
 4
 Phishing: Phishing is a technique through which hackers send fake login pages to your computer and mobile via mail, chat and popup ads that look exactly like the original login page
 aap jaise hi us login pej par apana yujar nem or password daalenge aapaki idi or password havers tah pahunch jaataa he or wo aasaani se aapkaa acount khol sakate hai
 How to avoid: To avoid phishing, whenever you open a website on the Internet, put HTTPS in front of the URL of the webpage
 aisa karne par phek log in pej aapke broujar main nahin khulegaa
 Do not open attachments of unknown emails and mark them as spam
 5
 Social media attack: Social media attack has become the most favorite way of hackers these days
 fasebuk, twitor,google plus jaise soshal media website par spam daalkar havers logon kii online activity ko read karke unasi juudi ahm jaankariyaan chori karte hai phir unhen edvertising agenciyon ko mote paison main bech dete hai
 How to avoid: Increase the privacy in your profile on social media
 anjaan vyakti kaa friend request except karne se bachein
 If you have a page on social media, use the keywords blocking method in it and block the suppers

 Hindutva is a part of the Indian way of life or is it religion? a seven-judge bench of the Supreme Court has initiated a review of the matter

 Can a person from one community ask for votes on the basis of their religion from the people of their community? Does it fall under the category of corrupt practices? Can a person from one community ask for votes from the people of his community for another candidate? Would it be a corrupt practice for a religious teacher to vote for someone else in the name of religion and the candidate's election should be canceled? darasal bharat main chunaav ke dauraan dharm, jati samudaay ityadi ke aadhaar par vot maangane yaa phir dharm guruon dwaara chunaav main kisi ko samarthan dekar dharm ke naam par vot daalane sambandhi taur tareeke kitne sahi or kitne galat hai? ise lekar supreme court sunwaayee kar rahaa he
 The Supreme Court during the first hearing of the case has refused to make the Central Government a party at present
 chif justise ne centre sarkaar ko maamle main party banane sambandhi maang ko khaarij karte hue kaha ki yah ek chunaav yachika kaa maamla he, jo ki sidhe chunaav ayog se judaa he
 In this, the central government cannot be made a party
 darasal 1995 ke faisle main supreme court ne kaha tha ki 'hindutv' ke naam par vot maangane se kisi ummidavaar ko koi paayda nahin hota he

 The court had said that seeking votes in the name of Hindutva is not a corrupt practice and it is not a corruption under Section 123 of the Representation of People Act
 tippaniyan Counsel for the petitioner stated on Section-123 of the Representation of People Act and Section 3 that if a person seeks votes on the basis of varna, religion, caste, language and community, it is termed as wrong methods of election
 aisa maamla paae jane par doshi vyakti kaa puraa chunaav radd kar diya jaataa he
 Significantly, in the 1992 Maharashtra assembly elections were held
 us samay vahaan ke netaa manohar joshi ne bayaan diya tha ki maharashtra ko ve pehla hindu rajya banaaenge
 There was a dispute and in 1995 the Bombay High Court quashed the said election
 phir yah maamla supreme court pahunchaa tha
 Later, a bench of Justice JS Verma in the Supreme Court ruled that Hindutva is a way of life, it could not be combined with Hinduism and overturned the judgment of the Bombay High Court
 2002 main maamle ko vichaar ke liye saat jajon kii sanvaidhanik peeth ko bheja gaya tha
